<script>
	$('#level1_select').change(function(){
		var val1 = $(this).val();
		if(val1 != ""){
			$('#level2_select option:not(.empty-val)').removeClass('show-option').addClass('hide-option');
			$('#level2_select option[data-level1="'+val1+'"').removeClass('hide-option').addClass('show-option');
		}else {
			$('#level2_select option:not(.empty-val)').removeClass('show-option').addClass('hide-option');
		}
		$('#level3_select option:not(.empty-val)').removeClass('show-option').addClass('hide-option');
		$('#level2_select option.empty-val').prop('selected', true);
		$('#level3_select option.empty-val').prop('selected', true);
		
	});

	$('#level2_select').change(function(){
		var val2 = $(this).val();
		let url = $(this).find('option:selected').attr('data-link');
		if(val2 != ""){
			
			$('#level3_select option:not(.empty-val)').removeClass('show-option').addClass('hide-option');
			$('#level3_select option[data-level2="'+val2+'"').removeClass('hide-option').addClass('show-option');
			let abc = $('#level3_select option[data-level2="'+val2+'"').length;
			if(abc == 0) {
				setTimeout(function(){
					window.location.href= url;
				}, 3000);
			}else {

			}
		}
		$('#level3_select option.empty-val').prop('selected', true);
		
	});

	$('#level3_select').change(function(){
		var val3 = $(this).val();
		if(val3 !='') {
			var url = $(this).find('option:selected').attr('data-link');
			//console.log(url);
			window.location.href= url;
		}
	});
</script>
